[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2906[0m[39m:            out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m0x10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m & [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2907[0m[39m:            out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m0x18[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m & [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2908[0m[39m:            in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2909[0m[39m:            out += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2910[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2911[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2912[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2913[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39min-instart > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2914[0m[39m:        ret = out - outstart;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2915[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2916[0m[39m:    *outlen = out - outstart;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2917[0m[39m:    *inlen = in - instart;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2918[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2919[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `UTF32ToUTF8` function in src/libxml2/encoding.c writes output bytes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout any checks on the remaining space in the provided output buffer. This [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39momission allows a small over-write [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte in the reported crash[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when the buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturned by `xmlBufCreate` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia the fuzz allocator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is just exactly filled or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnearly filled.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other conversion routines in encoding.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., UCS-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m to UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m define an [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`outend` pointer and guard each multi-byte write against `outend - out`, but [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UTF32ToUTF8` does not.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In UTF32ToUTF8 [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2843[0m[39m in encoding.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, introduce an `outend` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer computed from the incoming `*outlen` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich is the buffer capacity passed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the caller[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Before each write of [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m, or [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes into `out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, insert a bounds check [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the form  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < N[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      where N is the number of bytes the code is about to write.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Preserve the existing logic for setting `ret`, advancing `in` and `out` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointers, and reporting consumed/produced lengths at function exit.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/libxml2/encoding.c` and locate the function signature for [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UTF32ToUTF8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2843[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Directly after  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        unsigned long int b0, b1, b2, b3, c, d;  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      insert:  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        int maxOut = *outlen;  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        unsigned char *outend = out + maxOut;  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. In the loop starting at `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39min < inend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`, edit each write-case as [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollows:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Case c < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Case c < [0m[1;36m0x800[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Case [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0xF800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0xD800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Surrogate-pair case [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Retain the existing `in += [0m[33m...[0m[39m; out += [0m[33m...[0m[39m;` operations and final assignments[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *outlen = out - outstart;  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *inlen  = in  - instart;  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      so that callers still see the number of bytes consumed and produced.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Rebuild the library and run the full test suite plus the HTML parser fuzz [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness to confirm:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The original heap-buffer-overflow no longer reproduces.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No regressions occur in other encoding conversions.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Preservation of Functionality  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding explicit bounds checks mirrors the pattern used elsewhere in encoding.c[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2809[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2819[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlEncInputChunk` via `xmlCharEncInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supply `*outlen` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas the available buffer capacity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom `xmlBufAvail`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Using that value to compute [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`outend` ensures we do not overstep the allocation.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch does not alter any harness, fuzz, or test code; all existing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehaviors [0m[1;39m([0m[39merror codes, partial conversion on space exhaustion[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are preserved.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The extra branch checks incur minimal runtime overhead during conversion.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change to public APIs or error-handling contracts.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By breaking out of the loop when space runs out and returning the number of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes successfully written, callers still see a non-negative `ret`, leading to a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclean short-circuit rather than undefined memory corruption.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference for Similar Logic  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - See the preceding UCS-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m conversion in the same file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2809[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m2819[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefines `outend` and uses `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < neededBytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;`. The proposed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch reuses that proven approach.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
